“Fiscal Year” means a period of twelve consecutive months commencing on the first day of January 
of any year and ending on the last day of Decembe r of the same year, both inclusive; or such other 
consecutive twelve-month period as may hereafter be established as the fiscal year of the City for budgeting 
and accounting purposes to be evidenced, for purposes of the Trust Agreement, by a Certificate of an officer 
of the City filed with the Trustee. 
“Funds” and “Subfunds” means the Funds and Subfunds established or provided for pursuant to 
the Trust Agreement. 
“GAAP” means generally accepted accounting principles for entities such as the City as prescribed 
by (i) the pronouncements of the American Institute of Certified Public Accountants  and (ii) the Financial 
Accounting Standards Board and the Governmental Accounting Standards Board, as applicable. 
“General Bond Ordinance” means the Ordinance No. 29-16, passed by the Council on January 25, 
2016, and constituting a part of the Master Trust Agreement. 
“Government Certificates” means evidences of ow nership of proportionate interest in future 
interest or principal payments of Government Ob ligations, including depository receipts thereof.  
Investments in such proportionate interest must be limited to circumstances wherein (i) a bank or trust 
company acts as custodian and holds the underlying Government Obligations; (ii) the owner of the 
investment is the real party in interest and has the right to proceed directly and individually against the 
obligor of the underlying Government Obligations; and (iii) the underlying Government Obligations are 
held in a special account, segregated from the custodia n’s general assets, and are not available to satisfy 
any claim of the custodian, any person claiming through the custodian, or any person to whom the custodian 
may be obligated. 
“Government Obligations” means direct and gene ral obligations of, or obligations the timely 
payment of principal and interest on which are unconditionally guaranteed by, the United States of America. 
“Interest Commencement Date” means with respect to any Compound Interest and Income Bond, 
an Interest Payment Date prior to the scheduled maturity date for such Bond, as set forth in or pursuant to 
the Supplemental Bond Ordinance authorizing the issuance of such Bonds, after which interest accruing on 
such Bonds will be payable on each Interest Payment Da te, with the first such payment beginning on the 
applicable Interest Payment Date immediately succeeding such Interest Commencement Date. 
“Interest Payment Dates” means, with respect to any Series of Bonds, any date on which interest is 
due on such Bonds pursuant to the Supplemental Bond Ordinance authorizing the issuance of such Bonds. 
“Interest Rate Hedge Agreement” means an interest rate swap, an interest rate cap or other such 
arrangement obtained by the City, in accordance with appli cable law in effect at the time, with the goal of 
(i) lowering the effective interest rate to the City on Bonds; (ii) hedging the exposure of the City with 
respect to its obligations on Bonds against fluctuations in prevailing interest rates; (iii) otherwise reducing 
risk (including, without limitation, in addition to interest rate risk, tax risk or liquidity renewal risk) or 
otherwise managing exposure to changing markets (including, without limitation, in advance of issuances 
B-8of Bonds); (iv) achieving a more appropriate matc hing of its assets and liabilities; and (v) otherwise 
pursuing an optimal capital structure. 
“Mandatory Redemption Dates” means, with respect to any Series of Bonds, the dates, if any, on 
which such Bonds are required to be redeemed pursuant to the Supplemental Bond Ordinance authorizing 
the issuance of such Bonds. 
“Master Trust Agreement” means the Trust Agreement authorized pursuant to the General Bond 
Ordinance, to be entered into by the City and the Trustee. 
“Mayor” means the Mayor of the City and any Person succeeding to the powers, duties or functions 
of such office with respect to the General Bond Ordinance or the Bonds. 
“Net Revenues” means the Revenues in any Fiscal Year or other specified period net of Operating 
Expenses for that period. 
“Net Revenues Available for Debt Service” means, for purposes of satisfying the Additional Bonds 
Test and the Rate Covenant, Net Revenues for any period, excluding (i) proceeds from any insurance, other 
than business interruption insurance, or condemnation award, (ii) any profit or loss on the sale or other 
disposition, not in the ordi nary course of business, of investments or fixed or capital assets, (iii) any gift, 
grant or contribution or other such extraordinary and non-recurring item, (iv) proceeds of Bonds or 
Subordinated Indebtedness; (v) revenues resulting from th e early extinguishment of debt; and (vi) interest 
earnings on or credited to the Construction Fund. 
“Operating Expenses” means the operating expenses of the City for the System in any Fiscal Year 
or other specified period but excluding any allowance fo r depreciation, principal amortization and interest 
(whether on capitalized leases or other debt), and accrued unfunded pension and other post-employment 
benefit liabilities, all as determined (except as otherwi se specified in this definition) in accordance with 
GAAP for entities such as the City consistently applied.

to General Bond Ordinance.

“Outstanding Bonds” or “Bonds Outstanding” or “O utstanding” with respect to Bonds means all

under the Trust Agreement, except:  (i) Bonds surrendere d for exchange or registration of transfer and 
cancelled or cancelled because of payment or redemption on or prior to such date; (ii) Bonds (or the portions

deposited on or prior to such date with the Trustee or any Paying Agents (whether upon or prior to the 
maturity or redemption date of any such Bonds), or which are deemed to have been paid and discharged 
pursuant to the provisions of the Trust Agreement; provided that if such Bonds are to be redeemed prior to 
the maturity thereof, notice of such  redemption must have been given or arrangements satisfactory to the 
Trustee must have been made therefor, or waiver of such notice satisfactory in form to the Trustee must 
have been filed with the Trustee, and provided fu rther that if such Bonds are to be purchased for 
cancellation, a firm offer for sale stating the price h as been received and accepted; and (iii) lost, stolen, 
mutilated or destroyed Bonds in lieu of or in exchange for which others have been authenticated (or payment 
of which, when due, is made without replacement) unde r the Trust Agreement; provided, however, that in 
determining whether the Holders of the requisite pr incipal amount of Outstanding Bonds have given any 
B-9request, demand, authorization, direction, notice, consent or waiver under the Trust Agreement, Bonds 
owned by the City will be disregarded and deemed not to be Outstanding. 
“Parity Swap Obligations” means the portion of the payment obligations of the City under any 
Interest Rate Hedge Agreement that (i) represents the equivalent of interest on the notional amount of the 
Interest Rate Hedge Agreement (but does not represent, among other things, any termination payment that 
may be payable by the City thereunder),  and (ii) pursuant to the General Bond Ordinance, is secured by a 
pledge of Net Revenues on a parity with the pledge of Net Revenues that secures the Bonds.

trust company that may at any time be substituted in their place pursuant to the Trust Agreement and will 
also mean the Trustee where the context permits. 
“Person” or words importing persons means firms,  associations, partnerships (including without 
limitation, general and limited partnerships), joint ventures, societies, estates, trusts, corporations, public or 
governmental bodies, other legal entities and natural persons. 
“Predecessor Bond” of any particular Bond means every previous Bond evidencing all or a portion 
of the same debt as that evidenced by the particular Bond.  For the purposes of this definition, any Bond 
authenticated and delivered under the Master Trust Agr eement in lieu of a lost, stolen or destroyed Bond

Bond Ordinance. 
“Subordinated Indebtedness” means any obligation or evidence of indebtedness incurred by the 
City in accordance with the Trust Agreement, the debt service charges on which are payable and secured 
on a basis subordinate to the Debt Service on the B onds.  Without limiting the generality of the previous 
B-11sentence, “Subordinated Indebtedness” may include any obl igations payable by the City under an Interest 
Rate Hedge Agreement that are not Parity Swap Ob ligations. An obligation of the City need not be 
evidenced by a Supplemental Trust Agreement or expressly secured by the Trust Agreement for such 
obligation to qualify as Subordinated In debtedness or for the holders thereof to be entitled to payment of 
debt service charges thereon to be paid from the Subordinated Debt Service Fund.

including all Waste Water Facilities thereof, as extant  or as that system may be hereafter modified, 
improved, supplemented or extended. 
“Tax-Exempt Bonds” means any Bonds issued with an opinion of Bond Counsel that the interest 
thereon is excluded or excludible from gross income for purposes of federal income taxation. 
“Term Bonds” means the Bonds of any Series maturing on one principal maturity date, the principal 
of which is payable from fixed amounts required to be deposited in each year in the applicable Debt Service 
Fund for the payment of such principal on or prior to maturity.

Trustee under or pursuant to the Trust Agreement. 
“Variable Rate Bond” means any Bond that does no t bear interest throughout its term at a fixed 
rate, but that does bear interest at a rate that, during part or the entirety of the term of such Bond, varies 
from time to time based upon a formula or other method of determination set forth in the applicable 
Supplemental Bond Ordinance or Supplemental Trust Agreement.  If the rate of interest on any Bond that 
had been a Variable Rate Bond becomes fixed for the balance of the period until its maturity, that Bond 
will cease to be a Variable Rate Bond.  A Bond will not  be deemed a Variable Rate Bond solely because 
the rate of interest thereon may be adjusted if such interest becomes includable in gross income for purposes 
of federal income taxation. 
“Waste Water Facilities” means facilities for the pur pose of treating, neutra lizing, disposing of,

foregoing, facilities for the treatment and disposal of sewage or industrial waste and the residue thereof, 
facilities for the temporary or permanent impoundment of waste water, both surface and underground, and 
B-12storm and sanitary sewers and other systems, whether on the surface or underground, designed to transport 
waste water, together with the equipment and furn ishings thereof and their appurtenances and systems, 
whether on the surface or underground, including for ce mains and pumping facilities therefor when 
necessary. 
“Working Capital Reserve” means a reasonable reser ve for working capital, as determined by the 
City, not to exceed one-sixth of the Operating Expenses incurred during the preceding Fiscal Year.  
“Working Capital Reserve Subfund” means the Subf und of that name estab lished in the Revenue 
Fund pursuant to the General Bond Ordinance. 
The following is a summary of certain of the terms and provisions of the Trust Agreement. 
Pledge of and Lien on Net Revenues and Special Funds 
The City pledges and grants a lien on all Net Revenues and on moneys and securities on deposit in 
the Special Funds to secure the payment of the Bond Service Charges. 
Funds and Subfunds 
The City establishes and creates the following special trust funds and subfunds.
