The Trustee will establish (i) separate subaccounts in  the Interest Subfund and Principal Subfund 
of the Debt Service Fund for each Series of Bonds, (ii) separate subaccounts in the Debt Service Reserve 
Fund for any and each Series of Bonds to which the Debt Service Reserve Fund applies, (iii) separate 
subaccounts in the Construction Fund for each Series of Bonds with proceeds required to be deposited in 
the Construction Fund. 
The Revenue Fund and the Subfunds therein, the Contingency Fund and the Rate Stabilization Fund 
each will be held by the City and not commingled with other moneys of  the City except for purposes of 
investment.  The Debt Service Fund, Debt Service Reserve Fund, Construction Fund and Rebate Fund each 
B-13will be held by the Trustee.  The Subordinated Debt Service Fund will be held by the City or by the Trustee 
or such trustee or other party as may be specified in the trust agreement or other contract between the City 
and the holder or holders of the Subordinated Indebtedness.  All moneys or securities deposited with the 
Trustee pursuant to the Trust Agreement will be held  in trust and applied only in accordance with the 
provisions of the Trust Agreement and will be cons idered trust funds for the purposes of the Trust 
Agreement. 
Construction Fund 
There will be deposited from time to time in the Construction Fund the portion of the proceeds of 
the Bonds required to be deposited therein by any Supplemental Bond Ordinance and Supplemental Trust 
Agreement.  Amounts in the Construction Fund will be  expended only to pay Capital Costs and Costs of 
Issuance or to cure any deficiency in the Debt Service Fund or the Debt Service Reserve Fund following 
the deposits required, as described under “Revenue Fund,” which follows. 
Revenue Fund 
The City is required to cause all cash receipts that constitute Revenues of the System to be deposited 
into the Revenue Fund, along with any amounts that the City elects to transfer to the Revenue Fund from 
the Rate Stabilization Fund.  The amounts in the Revenue Fund will be deposited in the Operating Subfund 
and first applied to the payment of Operating Expenses;  thereafter, the balance in the Revenue Fund up to 
the Working Capital Reserve will be  deposited in the Working Capital Reserve Subfund and retained as a 
reserve for the payment of Operating Expenses and u sed for that purpose if the Operating Subfund will 
have been fully expended; and thereafter, the balance in the Revenue Fund will be paid at the times and in 
the amounts as follows: 
(A) To the Trustee for deposit in the Debt Service Fund as follows: 
1. Monthly, on or before the last day of ea ch month, the City will pay to the Trustee, 
for deposit in each subaccount in the Interest Subfund in the Debt Service Fund, an amount equal to one-
sixth of the amount of interest due on the next Interest Payment Date on the Outstanding Bonds of the Series 
to which such subaccount relates; provided, however, that if fewer than six months precede the next Interest 
Payment Date, then, on or before the last day of each such month an amount that, if deposited in each such 
month, would equal the amount of interest due on the next Interest Payment Date on the Outstanding Bonds 
of the Series to which such subaccount relates will be deposited therein; provided further, however, such 
monthly payments need be made only to the extent that the amount then on deposit in any such subaccount 
is less than the amount required to be on deposit therein in accordance herewith; and provided yet further, 
however, that the frequency and amou nt of any deposits required by th is paragraph will be subject to 
adjustment pursuant to the requirements of the Gene ral Bond Ordinance to make the deposits required for 
any Series of Bonds or any Parity Swap Obligations no less frequent than those for any other Series. 
2. Monthly, on or before the last day of each of the twelve months that precede a 
month in which a Serial Maturity Date occurs or a Sinking Fund Installment is due, the City will pay to the 
Trustee for deposit in each applicable subaccount in the Principal Subfund in the Debt Service Fund an 
amount equal to one-twelfth of the amount necessary to provide for the payment of the principal due on the 
next Serial Maturity Date or of the next Sinking Fund  Installment; provided, however, that if fewer than 
twelve months precede the next month in which a Serial Maturity Date occurs or a Sinking Fund Installment 
is due, then, on or before the last day of each such month an amount that, if deposited in each such month, 
would equal the amount of principal due on the next Se rial Maturity Date or of the next Sinking Fund 
Installment for the Outstanding Bonds of the Series to which such subaccount relates will be deposited 
therein; provided further, however, such monthly payments need be made only to the extent that the amount 
B-14then on deposit in any such subaccount is less than the amount required to be on deposit therein in 
accordance herewith; and provided yet further, howev er, that the frequency and amount of any deposits 
required by this paragraph will be subject to adjustment pursuant to the requirements of the General Bond 
Ordinance to make the deposits required for any Seri es of Bonds or any Parity Swap Obligations no less 
frequent than those for any other Series. 
(B) To the Trustee for deposit in the Debt Service Reserve Fund, monthly on or before the last 
day of each month, commencing on the date set forth in the applicable Supplemental Bond Ordinance with 
respect to any Series of Bonds for which the Debt Se rvice Reserve Requirement is to be deposited in the 
Debt Service Reserve Fund, the City must pay to th e Trustee for deposit in the subaccount established in 
the Debt Service Reserve Fund for such Series of A dditional Bonds, an amount such that, if that same 
amount were deposited in equal mont hly installments, the aggregate of the amounts so deposited in such 
subaccount would be equal to the Debt Service Reser ve Requirement with respect to such Series of 
Additional Bonds on the fifth (5th) anniversary of su ch commencement date, after giving effect to any 
amounts already on deposit therein and pledged to such  Series of Additional Bonds.  Thereafter, if the 
amount on deposit in such subaccount at any time is less than the Debt Service Reserve Requirement with 
respect to such Series of Additional Bonds, the City must pay to the Trustee for deposit in such subaccount, 
on or before the last day of each month following th e date of such deficiency, an amount equal to one-
twelfth of such deficiency.  The frequency and amount of any deposits required by this paragraph will be 
subject to adjustment pursuant to the General B ond Ordinance so that the deposits required by the 
provisions summarized by this paragraph for any Series of Bonds will be no less frequent than the deposits 
required by paragraph (A) above for Bond Service Charges or Parity Swap Obligations. 
(C) To any custodians of the Subordinated Debt Service Fund for deposit therein, such amounts 
as are required to be deposited therein on such dates as are specified in the Supplemental Trust Agreement 
or other contracts between the City and the holder or holders of the Subordinated Indebtedness.  If any 
Supplemental Trust Agreement or other contract between the City and the holder or holders of Subordinated 
Indebtedness requires the establishment and funding a reserve account related to such Subordinated 
Indebtedness, then any required deposits to such reserve account may be made after any otherwise required 
deposits described by this paragra ph (C) but before any required depos its described under paragraphs (D) 
and (E), below. 
(D) To the Contingency Fund, monthly on or before the l ast day of each month on which the 
balance in the Contingency Fund is less than the Contingency Fund Requirement, not less than 1/12 of the 
amount by which the Contingency Fund Requirement exceeds the balance. 
(E) To the Rate Stabilization Fund, on any date  on which deposits are required to be made by 
the provisions described in paragraphs (A) through (D), above, and after all such deposits are made, any 
amounts that the City elects to make to the Rate Stabilization Fund. 
(F) On the first day of each Fiscal Year or on th e first practicable date thereafter, the City will 
deposit any balance remaining in the Operating Subf und and the Working Capital Reserve Subfund in 
excess of the Working Capital Reserve at the end of th e preceding Fiscal Year to the credit of the Balance 
Subfund; provided, that the City may at any time provide for semiannual or quarterly deposits of such Net 
Revenues to the Balance Subfund. 
(G) Upon receipt of any Direct Payment, the C ity or the Trustee will cause it to be deposited 
(i) in the appropriate subaccount in the Debt Service Fund if such Direct Payment relates to Bonds, and 
(ii) in the appropriate account in the Subordinated De bt Service Fund if such Direct Payment relates to 
Subordinated Indebtedness, and will cause it to be a pplied solely to the purposes to which the Trust 
Agreement permits funds in such subaccount and account to be applied. 
B-15Debt Service Fund 
The Trustee will pay out of the applicable subaccounts in the Interest Subfund and in the Principal 
Subfund in the applicable Debt Service Fund to each Paying Agent (i) on or before each Interest Payment 
Date for the Bonds of each Series (x) the amount required for the interest payable on all such Outstanding 
Bonds on such date and (y) the amount, if any, required for the payment of the principal maturing on all 
such Outstanding Bonds on such date, and (ii) on or before the day preceding the redemption date for any 
such Bonds to be redeemed at the option of the City, the amount required for the payment of such Bonds 
then to be redeemed.  Such amounts will be so a pplied by each Paying Agent on and after the due date 
thereof. 
The City will pay to the Trustee for deposit in the Debt Service Fund any moneys held in any other 
Funds or Subfunds in excess of the amounts required to be  maintained therein that the City has elected to 
apply to the redemption prior to maturity of any Bonds, and such amounts will be so applied by the Trustee 
in the manner and at the times provided in the Trust Agreement. 
Amounts in the applicable subaccount in the Prin cipal Subfund for the payment of any Sinking 
Fund Installment for the Term Bonds of any Seri es then Outstanding (together with amounts in the 
applicable subaccount in the Interest Subfund with respect to the Term Bonds for which such Sinking Fund 
Installment was established) will be applied by the Trustee to the redemption of Term Bonds of the Series 
and maturity for which such Sinki ng Fund Installment was established in an amount not exceeding that 
necessary to effect the mandatory redemption of such  Term Bonds on the Mandato ry Redemption Dates.  
The Trustee will, by giving notice as provided in the Trust Agreement, proceed to call for redemption on 
the due date of any such Sinking Fund Installment the Term Bonds of the Series and maturity for which 
such Sinking Fund Installment w as established (except in the case of Term Bonds maturing on a Sinking 
Fund Installment date), in such amount as will be necessary to effect the mandatory redemption of such 
Term Bonds on the Mandatory Redemption Date in an amount equal to the amount of such Sinking Fund 
Installment.  The principal amount of Term Bonds of such Series and maturity theretofore delivered by the 
City to the Trustee to satisfy such Sinking Fund Inst allment, in the manner and to the extent as may be 
provided for in the General Bond Ordinance or in the Supplemental Bond Ordinance or Supplemental Trust 
Agreement authorizing such Series, will be credited against the amount of such Sinking Fund Installment.  
Such notice will be given regardless of whether or no t moneys therefor will have  been deposited in the 
Principal Subfund in the applicable Debt Service Fund and without any instructions of the City.  The Trustee 
will pay out of the Principal Subfund in the applicable Debt Service Fund to the appropriate Paying Agent, 
on or before the day preceding such Mandatory Redemption Date, the amount required for the redemption 
of the Term Bonds so called for redemption, and such amount will be applied by such Paying Agent to such 
redemption.  All expenses in connection with such redemption of Term Bonds will be paid by the City from 
the Operating Subfund. 
To the extent that a Series of Bonds is secured by credit enhancement or liquidity support provided 
by a Credit Provider pursuant to a Reimbursement Ag reement, the Supplemental Bond Ordinance and 
Supplemental Trust Agreement with respect to that Series may provide that the Trustee will apply amounts 
in the Debt Service Fund first, to the payment of Bo nd Service Charges and any Parity Swap Obligations 
then due and, second, to the payment of any Credit Obligations then due. 
B-16Debt Service Reserve Fund 
If on any Interest Payment Date, the amount in th e subaccount in the Interest Subfund or the 
Principal Subfund for any Series of Bonds is less than the amount required to be therein on deposit pursuant 
to the Trust Agreement, the Trustee will, after any required deposits to Subordinated Debt Service Fund, 
Contingency Fund, Rate Stabilization Fund and Ba lance Subfund are made, apply the amounts in the 
applicable Subfund, if any, in the Debt Service Reserve Fund to the extent necessary to make good any 
such deficiency (or the entire amount in the applicable Subfund if less than sufficient).  The City may, so 
long as it will not result in a reduction of the rating assi gned to any of the Bonds, substitute for funds on 
deposit in the Debt Service Reserve Fund a letter of credit, surety bond or other credit enhancement facility 
issued by a Qualified Financial Institution. 
Subordinated Debt Service Fund 
If on the third day before any Interest Payment Date, the amount in any of the Subfunds in the Debt 
Service Fund is less than the amount required to be on deposit therein pursuant to the General Bond 
Ordinance, after deposits, if any, are made to the Co ntingency Fund, Rate Stabilization Fund and Balance 
Subfund, the City will, upon the request of the Trust ee, transfer or cause the transfer of moneys from the 
Subordinated Debt Service Fund to the Trustee to make good any such deficiency (or the entire amount in 
the Subordinated Debt Service Fund if less than sufficient). 
If on any day next following the date of a payment and deposit required into a Debt Service Reserve 
Fund, the amount in any of the Subfunds in the Debt Service Reserve Fund is less than the amount required 
to be on deposit therein, the City will, upon the request of the Trustee, transfer moneys from the 
Subordinated Debt Service Fund to the Trustee for depos it in the appropriate Subfund in the Debt Service 
Reserve Fund an amount sufficient to cure any such deficiency (or the entire amount in the Subordinated 
Debt Service Fund if less than sufficient). 
Subject to the provisions described in the two preceding paragraphs and the provisions relating to 
the Rebate Fund, the amounts on deposit in the Subo rdinated Debt Service Fund will be applied to the 
payment of the principal of and interest and any premium on Subordinated Indebtedness as and when due 
or to the required funding of any special reserve account established for any Subordinated Indebtedness. 
Contingency Fund 
If on the third day before any Interest Payment Date, the amount in any of the Subfunds in the Debt 
Service Fund is less than the amount required to be on deposit therein pursuant to the General Bond 
Ordinance, after deposits, if any, are made to the Rate Stabilization Fund and the Balance Subfund, the City 
will, upon the request of the Trustee, transfer or cau se the transfer of moneys from the Contingency Fund 
to the Trustee to the extent necessary to make good any such deficiency (or the entire amount in the 
Contingency Fund if less than sufficient). 
If on any day next following the date of a payment and deposit required into the Debt Service 
Reserve Fund, the amount in any of the Subfunds in the Debt Service Reserve Fund is less than the amount 
required to be on deposit therein pursuant to the Gene ral Bond Ordinance, the City will, upon the request 
of the Trustee, transfer moneys from the Contingenc y Fund to the Trustee for deposit in the appropriate 
Subfund in the Debt Service Reserve Fund an amount sufficient to cure any such deficiency (or the entire 
amount in the Contingency Fund if less than sufficient). 
B-17Subject to the provisions described in the two proceeding paragraphs and the requirements of the 
General Bond Ordinance pertaining to the Rebate Fund, the amounts on deposit in the Contingency Fund 
may be used only for the payment of Capital Costs or for the purpose of redeeming Bonds. 
Rate Stabilization Fund 
If on the third day before any Interest Payment Date, the amount in any of the Subfunds in the Debt 
Service Fund is less than the amount required to be on deposit therein pursuant to the General Bond 
Ordinance, after deposits, if any, are made from the Balance Subfund, the City will, upon the request of the 
Trustee, transfer or cause the transfer of moneys fro m the Rate Stabilization Fund to the Trustee to make 
good any such deficiency (or the entire amount in the Rate Stabilization Fund if less than sufficient). 
If on any day next following the date of a payment and deposit required into the Debt Service 
Reserve Fund, the amount in any of the Subfunds in the Debt Service Reserve Fund is less than the amount 
required to be on deposit, the City will, upon the re quest of the Trustee, transfer moneys from the Rate 
Stabilization Fund to the Trustee for deposit in the appropriate Subfund in the Debt Service Reserve Fund 
an amount sufficient to cure any such deficiency (or the entire amount in the Rate Stabilization Fund if less 
than sufficient). 
Subject to the provisions described in the two preceding paragraphs and the provisions relating to 
the Rebate Fund, the City may from time to time transfer amounts on deposit in the Rate Stabilization Fund 
to the Revenue Fund and cause them to be applied as Revenues. 
Balance Subfund 
If on the third day before any Interest Payment Date, the amount in any of the Subfunds in the Debt 
Service Fund is less than the amount required to be on deposit in that fund, the City will, upon the request 
of the Trustee, transfer moneys from the Balance Subfund to the Trustee to make good any such deficiency 
(or the entire amount in the Subordinated Debt Service Fund if less than sufficient). 
If on any day next following a payment date, the amount in any of the Subfunds in the Debt Service 
Reserve Fund is less than the amount required to be on deposit in that fund, the City will, upon the request 
of the Trustee, transfer moneys from the Balance S ubfund to the Trustee for deposit in the appropriate 
Subfund in the Debt Service Reserve Fund an amount su fficient to cure any such deficiency (or the entire 
amount in the Balance Subfund if less than sufficient). 
Subject to the provisions described in the two immediately preceding paragraphs and the provisions 
described in the discussion of the Rebate Fund, below, the amounts on deposit in the Balance Subfund will 
be applied by the City to any lawful System purpo ses, including, but not limited to, transfers to the 
Subordinated Debt Service Fund for payment of the principal of and interest on any Subordinated 
Indebtedness and the funding or replenishment of any special reserve account established for any 
Subordinated Indebtedness, but amoun ts on deposit in the Balance Subfund may not be transferred or 
credited to the Rate Stabilization Fund. 
Rebate Fund 
The General Bond Ordinance establishes and orders to be maintained as a separate deposit account 
(except when invested) in the custody of the Trustee a Rebate Fund.  Any provision of the General Bond 
Ordinance or of the Trust Agreement to the contrary notwithstanding, the Rebate Fund is not pledged to the 
payment of Bond Service Charges, is not one of or pa rt of any of the Special Funds, and is free and clear 
B-18of any lien of the Trust Agreement.  Separate account s will be created in the Rebate Fund for each Series 
of Bonds. 
At least five days prior to the end of the fifth Bond Year and each fifth Bond Year thereafter for 
each Series of Bonds and within five days after the date on which all outstanding Bonds of such Series are 
paid or deemed paid in full, the City will calculate or will furnish information to and engage an independent 
certified public accounting firm that is not unacceptable to the Trustee, to calculate, the Rebate Amount as 
of the end of that Bond Year or the date of such final payment.  The Trustee may rely upon the City for the 
calculation of the Rebate Amount, provided that the Trustee receives a verification of the accuracy of such 
computations by a firm of independent certified public accountants or an opinion of nationally recognized 
bond counsel that such computations are in compliance with the Code.  Within 30 days after the end of the 
fifth Bond Year and every fifth Bond Year thereafter, the Trustee, acting on behalf of the City and at the 
written direction of the City, will pay to the United States in accordance with Section 148(f) of the Code 
from the moneys then on deposit in the applicable account in the Rebate Fund an amount equal to 90% (or 
such greater percentage not in excess of 100% as the City may direct the Trustee in writing to pay) of the 
Rebate Amount determined from the date of the origin al delivery of the Bonds of that Series (less the 
portion of the Rebate Amount, if any,  previously paid to the United States).  Within sixty (60) days after 
the payment in full of all outstanding Bonds of such Series and upon written direction of the City, the 
Trustee will pay to the United States in accordance with Section 148(f) of the Code from the moneys then 
on deposit in the applicable account in the Rebate Fund an amount equal to 100% of the Rebate Amount 
determined from the date of the original delivery of th e Bonds of that Series to the date of such payment 
(but less that portion of the Rebate Amount, if any, pr eviously paid to the United States) and any moneys 
remaining in the applicable account in the Rebate Fund following such payment will be paid to the City.  
Notwithstanding anything in the General Bond Ordina nce to the contrary, the moneys needed for any 
payment required by the preceding two sentences may be derived from balances in any of the Special Funds 
other than the Debt Service Fund and the Debt Servi ce Reserve Fund, and the City agrees to apply those 
balances to that purpose in the following Order: the Balance Subfund, the Rate Stabilization Fund, the 
Contingency Fund, the Subordinate d Indebtedness Fund and any relate d reserve fund or account, and the 
Construction Fund. 
Investment of Funds and Subfunds 
Moneys held in the Debt Service Reserve Fund or in any special reserve account established for 
any Series of Bonds will be invested and reinvested, in accordance with written instructions received from 
the City, by the Trustee, to the fullest extent practicable, in Eligible Investments maturing not later than the 
final maturity of the Series of Bonds for which the applicable subaccount was established or subject to 
withdrawal at any time required for purposes of the Debt Service Reserve Fund. 
Moneys held in the Debt Service Fund will be invested and reinvested, in accordance with written 
instructions from the City, by the Trustee, to the full est extent possible, in Eligible Investments maturing 
within one year from the date of purchase but in an y event not later than such times as is necessary to 
provide moneys for required payments to be made from such Funds or subject to withdrawal at any such 
time. 
Except as otherwise provided in the General Bond Ordinance with respect to  the investment of 
moneys in the Debt Service Fund and the Debt Se rvice Reserve Fund or any special reserve account 
established for any Series of Bonds, and only to the exte nt otherwise provided, moneys held in the Funds 
and Subfunds are invested and reinvested by the City  and the Trustee, as the case may be, to the fullest 
extent practicable, in Eligible Investments that mature or are subject to withdrawal not later than such times 
as are necessary to provide moneys for payments to be made from such Funds and Subfunds, as required 
by the General Bond Ordinance and in the applicable Supplemental Bond Ordinance or Supplemental Trust 
B-19Agreement; provided, however, that the Trustee may make such investments only in accordance with 
instructions received from the City. 
An investment that can be red eemed at the option of the holder or that may be sold at a pre-
established price to a “Qualified Purchase Agreement Provider” (as hereinafter defined) pursuant to a 
written agreement within a specified time period will be deemed to mature within that specified time period 
for purposes of limitations in the General Bond Ordina nce on the maximum maturity of investments, but 
only for as long as the redemption or sale option remains exercisable within the specified period.  A 
“Qualified Purchase Agreement Provider” means a financ ial institution, including, without limitation, a 
bank (including the Trustee or any of it s affiliates) or insurance company) that is rated, or the obligations 
of which are rated, in one of the top two rating categories by at least two Rating Agencies. 
In computing the amount in any Fund or Subfund established under the provisions of the General 
Bond Ordinance, obligations purchased as an investment of moneys therein will be valued at the lower of 
market value or the amortized value thereof.  Amorti zed value, when used with respect to an obligation 
purchased at par, means the par amount thereof, and, when used with respect to an obligation purchased at 
a premium above or a discount below par, means the value as of any given time obtained by dividing the 
total premium or discount at which such obligation was purchased by the number of interest payments 
remaining on such obligation after such purchase and deducting the amount thus calculated for each interest 
payment date after such purchase from the purchase price in the case of an obligation purchased at a 
premium and adding the amount thus calculated for each interest payment date after such purchase to the 
purchase price in the case of an obligation purchased at a discount. 
Except as otherwise provided in the General Bond Ordinance, the Trustee will sell at the best price 
obtainable, using reasonable diligence to determine such best price, or present for redemption, any 
obligation so purchased as an investment whenever it is so requested in writing by the Director of Finance 
or whenever it is necessary in order to provide moneys to meet any payment or transfer from any Fund held 
by it. 
Investments purchased as an investment of moneys in any Fund or Subfund will be deemed at all 
times to be a part of such Fund or Subfund, and any losses suffered due to the investment thereof will be 
charged to such Fund or Subfund.  A deficiency in a Subfund in the Debt Service Reserve Fund will not be 
deemed to exist as of a date of transfer if the am ount on deposit therein is less than the applicable Debt 
Service Reserve Requirement with respect to any Series of Bonds solely because as of such date of transfer 
one or more deposits to such Subfund in the Debt Service Reserve Fund is not required in connection with 
the original issuance of such Series until a future date or dates. 
The valuation and sale of investments may be am ended in the Master Trust Agreement or any 
Supplemental Trust Agreement upon the request of a Credit Provider. 
Authorization of the Issuance of Bonds 
The Trust Agreement authorizes the issuance from time to time of Bonds for the purpose only of 
paying Capital Costs, or refunding, including advance refunding, for any lawful purpose, any Outstanding 
Bonds or Subordinated Indebtedness,  where such refunding will not adversely affect the exclusion of the 
interest on any Tax-Exempt Bonds from gross income for the purposes of federal income tax. 
Upon the original issuance of Additional Bonds, th e City must deliver to the Trustee certain 
certifications, including the following: 
B-20(i) A Certificate of the Director of Finance and the Director of Law, certifying that, 
to their knowledge, the City is not, on the date  of issuance of the Bonds, in default in the 
performance of any of its covenants provided in  the General Bond Ordinance, in the Trust 
Agreement or in the Bonds; 
(ii) For any Series of Additional Bonds that the City issues for the payment of Capital 
Costs or for the purpose of refunding Subordinate d Indebtedness or other obligations other than 
Outstanding Bonds, either (A) a Certificate of th e Director of Finance certifying that the Net 
Revenues Available for Debt Service  for the preceding Fiscal Year or any consecutive 12 calendar 
months during the 18-month period immediately preceding the date of original issuance of the 
proposed Series of Bonds (in each case, the “Test Period”) are in an amount not less than the greater 
of (1) 120% of maximum annual Debt Service on all Bonds then Outstanding and on the proposed 
Series of Additional Bonds or (2) 100% of the sum of: (A) maximum annual Debt Service on any 
Bonds then Outstanding and on the proposed Series of Bonds, (B) all required deposits to the Debt 
Service Reserve Fund, (C) all required deposits to the Subordinated Debt Service Fund and to any 
reserve fund securing Subordinated Indebtedness, (D) all required deposits to the Contingency 
Fund, and (E) debt service payable on any other obligations payable from the Balance Subfund and 
deposits to any reserve funds securing such other obligations, during that Test Period (the amounts 
described in clauses (A) through (E) being referred to collectively as the “Test Amount”), or (B) a 
Certificate of the Director of Finance, which may be, but is not required to be, accompanied by or 
based upon a Certificate of a Consulting Engineer , certifying that the Adjusted Net Revenues for 
the Test Period are in an amount not less than the greater of (1) 120% of maximum annual Debt 
Service on any Bonds then Outstanding and on the proposed Series of Bonds or (2) 100% of the 
Test Amount during that Test Period.  No certif ication under the provision described in this 
paragraph is required for any Series of Bonds being issued for the purpose of refunding Outstanding 
Bonds, provided that the issuance of the refunding  Bonds will not result in any increase in Debt 
Service in any Fiscal Year; otherwise, the same certification is required as for a Series of Bonds for 
the payment of Capital Costs; and 
For purposes of determining the City’s compliance with the Additional Bonds Test, the amount of 
any Direct Payment received or expected to be received by the City or the Trustee in any Fiscal Year will 
be credited against (i) Debt Service in such Fiscal Year if such Direct Payment relates to Bonds or (ii) debt 
service on Subordinated Indebtedness in such Fiscal Year  if such Direct Payment relates to Subordinated 
Indebtedness.  
Bond Anticipation Notes .  In anticipation of the issuance of any Series of Additional Bonds, the 
City may issue one or more Series of Bond Anticipati on Notes.  All requirements of the Trust Agreement 
applicable to Bonds also apply to Bond Anticipation Notes, including, without limitation the conditions 
precedent for the issuance of a Series of Bonds.  Fo r the purpose of (i) determining compliance with the 
Rate Covenant for any period prior to the date of calculation, (ii) determining whether Additional Bonds 
may be issued in compliance with the requirement s with the Additional Bonds Test when any Bond 
Anticipation Notes are outstanding, (iii) determining whether Bond Anticipation Notes may be issued in 
compliance with the requirements of the Additional B onds Test, and (iv) determining the amount of the 
Debt Service Reserve Requirement attributable to such Bond Anticipation Notes, the Debt Service payable 
on any Bond Anticipation Notes will be computed for purposes of the Trust Agreement in accordance with 
the provisions of the Trust Agreement pertaining to  Balloon Bonds and described in the subsection below 
entitled “Balloon Bonds.” 
Debt Service Reserve Requirement .  In connection with any issuan ce of Bonds, the City may, in 
the applicable Supplemental Trust Agreement, provide that no deposit to the Debt Service Reserve Fund 
will be made for or with respect to such Additional Bonds, in which case:  (i) the holders of such Additional 
B-21Bonds will have no right or entitlement to have any portion of the Bond Service Charges on such Additional 
Bonds be paid from any amounts in the Debt Service Reserve Fund, (ii) the lien of and pledge on the Debt 
Service Reserve Fund will not extend to or be for th e benefit of the holders of such Bonds, and (iii) the 
Debt Service on such Bonds will not  be taken into account in determ ining the Debt Service Reserve 
Requirement. 
In the event that the Supplemental Trust Agreement applicable to an issue of Additional Bonds 
provides as described in the preceding paragraph, th en such Supplemental Trust Agreement may also 
provide for the creation of a special reserve account solely for such Bonds, separate from the Debt Service 
Reserve Fund, and may provide for the deposit therein, at the time of issuance or in one or more subsequent 
deposits thereto, of an amount specified in the applicable Supplemental Trust Agreement as the required 
reserve for such Bonds, or may require the City to provide a municipal bond insurance policy, a bank letter 
or line of credit, or any other form of credit or liqui dity facility issued by a Qualified Financial Institution 
to enhance the security for such Bonds in lieu of  a funded reserve account.  If the Supplemental Trust 
Agreement applicable to such a Series of Bonds so provides for such a special reserve account and further 
requires that deposits be made thereto from Net Reve nues at any time, then such deposits may be made 
only from moneys remaining in the Revenue Fund on the last day of a month after any required deposits to 
the Debt Service Reserve Fund. 
If the Supplemental Trust Agreement applicable to a Series of Bonds provides for no reserve 
account, or for a special reserve account as permitted by the preceding paragraph, then such Supplemental 
Trust Agreement must also provide that the amount of any defaulted principal of or interest on such Series 
of Bonds that would have been timely paid had the Debt Service Reserve Requirement for such Bonds been 
funded in the Debt Service Reserve Fund may be pa id only from moneys remaining in the Revenue Fund 
on the last day of a month after any required deposits to the Debt Service Reserve Fund. 
Computation of Debt Service With Respect to Bonds 
In the event that all or any portion of any Series of Bonds have been issued as or are proposed to 
be issued as Variable Rate Bonds, then, except as otherwise provided in the Trust Agreement, in order to 
compute the Debt Service on such Bonds for the purposes of the Trust Agreement, the following rules will 
apply: 
Variable Rate Bonds.  Regarding Variable Rate Bonds: 
(i) For the purpose of determining complian ce with the Rate Covenant for any period 
prior to the date of calculation, the rate of interest borne by any Outstanding Variable Rate Bonds 
will be deemed to be the actual weighted average rate in effect thereon during such period. 
(ii) For the purpose of determining whether Bonds may be issued in compliance with 
the Additional Bonds Test, regardless of whether su ch Bonds are to be Variable Rate Bonds, the 
rate of interest to be borne by any Outstanding Variable Rate Bonds will be deemed to be the 
highest rate of interest borne by such Variable Rate Bonds during the preceding 24 months, but if 
such Variable Rate Bonds have not been outst anding for 24 months preceding the date of the 
computation, then it is to be assumed that such Variable Rate Bonds will bear interest at a fixed 
interest rate equal to 120% of the highest rate applicable within the 24 months immediately 
preceding the date of the computation under an index generally accepted in the securities industry 
for securities having ratings and maturity or tender  dates comparable to those of the Outstanding 
Variable Rate Bonds. 
B-22(iii) For the purpose of determining whether Bonds that are to be Variable Rate Bonds 
may be issued in compliance with the Additiona l Bonds Test, and for the purpose of determining 
the amount of the Debt Service Reserve Requirement, if any, attributable to such Variable Rate 
Bonds, the rate of interest to be borne by such Variable Rate Bonds will be deemed to be a fixed 
interest rate equal to 120% of the highest rate applicable within the 24 months immediately 
preceding the date of the computation under an index generally accepted in the securities industry 
for securities having ratings and ma turity or tender dates comparab le to those of the proposed 
Variable Rate Bonds. 
(iv) For the purpose of determining whether any Outstanding Variable Rate Bond is 
deemed paid and discharged for purposes of the Trust Agreement, such Va riable Rate Bond will 
be deemed to bear interest at the actual rate of interest borne thereby for the remainder of the period 
that such rate remains in effect, and for any s ubsequent period prior to the date on which such 
Variable Rate Bond is actually to be paid and discharged, such Variable Rate Bond will be deemed 
to bear interest at the maximum rate of interest such Variable Rate Bond may bear pursuant to the 
Supplemental Trust Agreement applicable thereto. 
Balloon Bonds.  Regarding any Bonds that are or are proposed to be issued as Balloon Bonds, for 
the purpose of (i) determining compliance with the Ra te Covenant for any period prior to the date of 
calculation, (ii) determining whether Additional Bonds, regardless of whether they are to be Balloon Bonds, 
may be issued in compliance with the Additional Bonds Test when any Balloon Bonds are outstanding, (iii) 
determining whether Bonds that are to be Balloon Bonds may be issued in compliance with the Additional 
Bonds Test, and (iv) determining the amount of the Debt Service Reserve Requirement, if any, attributable 
to such Balloon Bonds, the Debt Service on such Bonds will be determined as follows: 
(A) if such Balloon Bonds are not Capital Appreciation Bonds, by assuming that such 
Balloon Bonds are to be amortized on the basis of level debt service over the Assumed Amortization 
Period and that such Bonds bear interest at the Assumed Interest Rate; and 
(B) if such Balloon Bonds are Capital Appreciation Bonds, by assuming that the 
Appreciated Principal Amount of such Bonds at maturity is to be amortized on the basis of level 
principal payments over the Assumed Amortization Period. 
Capital Appreciation Bonds.  Regarding any Bonds that are or are proposed to be issued as Capital 
Appreciation Bonds, for the purpose of (i) determining compliance with the Rate Covenant for any period 
prior to the date of calculation, (ii) determining whether Bonds, regardless of whether they are to be Capital 
Appreciation Bonds, may be issued in compliance w ith the Additional Bonds Test when any Capital 
Appreciation Bonds are outstanding, (iii) determining whether Bonds that are to be Capital Appreciation 
Bonds may be issued in compliance with the Addition al Bonds Test, and (iv) determining the amount of 
the Debt Service Reserve Requirement attributable to  such Capital Appreciation Bonds, the Debt Service 
on such Bonds will include the Appreciated Principal Amounts at maturity. 
Interest Rate Hedge Agreements .  If the City enters into an In terest Rate Hedge Agreement to 
simulate a fixed rate of interest on Variable Rate Bonds, then the City may (1) secure the portion of the 
payment obligations of the City thereunder that represents the equivalent of interest on the notional amount 
of the Interest Rate Hedge Agreement with a pledge of the Net Revenues on a parity with the pledge thereof 
that secures the Bonds, and (2) cause the debt structure that is simulated through the combination of the 
Variable Rate Bonds with such Interest Rate Hedge  Agreement to apply for purposes of calculating or 
projecting the Debt Service on such Variable Rate Bonds for any period of time during which such Interest 
Rate Hedge Agreement is to be effec tive, provided that (i) the debt structure that is simulated through the 
combination of the Variable Rate Bonds with such Interest Rate Hedge Agreement complies with the 
B-23restrictions of the Trust Agreement on the terms of an d security for the Bonds applied to that structure as 
though it consisted entirely of Bonds and as though th e portion of the payment obligations of the City 
thereunder that represents the equivalent of interest  on the notional amount of the Interest Rate Hedge 
Agreement payable to the counterparty to the Inte rest Rate Hedge Agreement constituted Bond Service 
Charges, (ii) the counterparty to any swap agreement and the provider of any interest rate cap is rated either 
of the two highest rating categories by at least two Rating Agencies, (iii) no such Interest Rate Hedge 
Agreement purports to entitle the counterparty to th e Interest Rate Hedge Agreement to payment by the 
City from any source other than the Net Revenues, bu t such Interest Rate He dge Agreement may provide 
for securing any portion of the payment obligations of the City thereunder that represents the equivalent of 
interest on the notional amount of the Interest Rate Hedge Agreement (but does not represent, among other 
things, any termination payment that may be payable by the City ther eunder) with a pledge of the Net 
Revenues on a parity with the pledge thereof that secures the Bonds; and (iv) the cost of obtaining such 
Interest Rate Hedge Agreement has been determined by the Director of Finance (who may obtain the written 
advice of a Financial Advisor) to be justified by the corresponding benefit to the City and to be 
commercially reasonable based on then current market conditions.  In the event th e City enters into any 
such Interest Rate Hedge Agreement, it may not exercise any option to terminate such Interest Rate Hedge 
Agreement unless the Variable Rate Bonds to which su ch Interest Rate Hedge Agreement had related and 
that will remain outstanding after the termination thereof would fulfill the requirements of the Trust 
Agreement as they apply to Variable Rate Bonds, as though such Variable Rate Bonds were being issued 
on the date of the termination of such Interest Rate Hedge Agreement.  If deposits to the Debt Service Fund 
for Parity Swap Obligations created pursuant this paragraph are required to be made more frequently than 
had been required for Bond Service Charges on any Outstanding Bonds, then, from and after the time such 
deposits for Parity Swap Obligations commence, deposits to the Debt Service Fund must be required for all 
Outstanding Bonds with the same frequency as they are required for such Parity Swap Obligations. 
If the City enters into an Interest Rate Hedge Agreement to simulate a variable rate of interest on 
fixed rate Bonds, then the City may (1) secure the portion of the payment obligations of the City thereunder 
that represents the equivalent of interest on the notional amount of the Interest Rate Hedge Agreement with 
a pledge of the Net Revenues on a parity with the pl edge thereof that secures the Bonds, and (2) cause the 
debt structure that is simulated through the combinati on of the fixed rate Bonds with such Interest Rate 
Hedge Agreement to apply for purposes of calculating or  projecting the Debt Service on such fixed rate 
Bonds for any period of time during which such Interest Rate Hedge Agreement is to be effective, provided 
that (i) the debt structure that is simulated through the combination of the fixed rate Bonds with such Interest 
Rate Hedge Agreement complies with the restrictions of the Trust Agreement on the terms of and security 
for the Bonds applied to that structure as though it consisted entirely of Variable Rate Bonds and as though 
the portion of the payment obligations of the City ther eunder that represents the equivalent of interest on 
the notional amount of the Interest Rate Hedge Agreement payable to the counterparty to the Interest Rate 
Hedge Agreement constituted Bond Service Charges, (ii)  the counterparty to any swap agreement and the 
provider of any interest rate cap is rated either of  the two highest rating categories by at least two Rating 
Agencies, (iii) no such Interest Rate Hedge Agreemen t purports to entitle the counterparty to the Interest 
Rate Hedge Agreement to payment by the City from any source other than the Net Revenues, but such 
Interest Rate Hedge Agreement may provide for securi ng any portion of the payment obligations of the 
City thereunder that represents the equivalent of interest on the notional amount of the Interest Rate Hedge 
Agreement (but does not represent, among other things, any termination payment that may be payable by 
the City thereunder) with a pledge of the Net Revenues on a parity with the pledge thereof that secures the 
Bonds; and (iv) the cost of obtaining such Interest  Rate Hedge Agreement has been determined by the 
Director of Finance (who may obtain the written advice of a financial advisor) to be justified by the 
corresponding benefit to the City and to be comme rcially reasonable based on then current market 
conditions.  In the event the City en ters into any such Interest Rate Hedge Agreement, it may  not exercise 
any opti
on to terminate such Interest Rate Hedge Agreement unless the fixed rate Bonds to which such 
Interest Rate Hedge Agreement had related and that will remain outsta nding after the termination thereof 
B-24would fulfill the requirements of the Trust Agreement as they apply to fixed rate Bonds, as though such 
fixed rate Bonds were being issued on the date of the termination of such Interest Rate Hedge Agreement.  
If deposits to the Debt Service Fund for Parity Sw ap Obligations created pursuant this paragraph are 
required to be made more frequently than had been required for Bond Service Charges on any Outstanding 
Bonds, then, from and after the time such deposits for Parity Swap Obligations commence, deposits to the 
Debt Service Fund must be required for all Outstanding Bonds with the same frequency as they are required 
for such Parity Swap Obligations. 
Covenants of the City 
The City covenants under the General Bond Ordinance with the Holders of the Bonds as follows: 
(i) The City will maintain the System, or will cause the System to be maintained, in 
sound operating condition and free from any liens or encumbrances which would interfere with the 
full and continuous use and operation thereof by the City. 
(ii) The City will keep proper books of reco rd and account so as to show the complete 
financial results of the operation of the Syst em, including Revenues and Operating Expenses and 
all capital expenditures therefor, and will invest and deposit cash receipts that constitute Revenues 
in accordance with applicable laws, the General Bond Ordinance and the Trust Agreement. 
(iii) The City will at all times prescribe, charge  and collect such rates, rentals and other 
charges for the use of the services of the System and must restrict the Operating Expenses of the 
System in such a way that Net Revenues Available for Debt Service (adjusted for purposes of clause 
(i) as described in the following sentence) in each Fiscal Year may be not less than the greater of 
(i) 120% of Debt Service on a ll Bonds then Outstanding payable during that Fiscal Year or (ii) 
100% of the sum of: (A) Debt Service on all Bonds then Outstanding payable during that Fiscal 
Year, (B) all required deposits to the Debt Serv ice Reserve Fund during that Fiscal Year, (C) all 
required deposits to the Subordinated Debt Se rvice Fund and to any reserve fund securing 
Subordinated Indebtedness during that Fiscal Year, (D) all required deposits to the Contingency 
Fund during that Fiscal Year, and (E) debt service payable on any other obligations payable from 
the Balance Subfund and deposits to any reserve funds securing such other obligations during that 
Fiscal Year.  For purposes of clause (i) of the preceding sentence, but not for the purpose of clause 
(ii) of the preceding sentence, “Net Revenues Available for Debt Service” for any Fiscal Year will 
include any amounts transferred from the Rate Stabilization Fund to the Revenue Fund during such 
Fiscal Year, but will be reduced by any amounts transferred from the Revenue Fund to the Rate 
Stabilization Fund during that period.  For purposes of determining the City’s compliance with the 
Rate Covenant, the amount of any Direct Payments received by the City or the Trustee in any Fiscal 
Year will be credited against (i) Debt Service in such Fiscal Year if such Direct Payment related to 
Bonds or (ii) debt service on Subordinated Indebtedness in such Fiscal Year if such Direct Payment 
related to Subordinated Indebtedness. 
(iv) If in any Fiscal Year the Net Revenues Av ailable for Debt Service is less than the 
amount required under paragraph (iii), above, the City will, within 30 days following receipt by the 
City of its audited annual financial statement and the written request of the Trustee, employ a 
Consulting Engineer to make recommendations with in 45 days as to a revision of the rates, fees 
and charges or Operating Expenses or methods of operation of the System, if any, that will result 
in producing the amount so required in the next  succeeding Fiscal Year.  The City covenants and 
agrees, promptly upon its receipt of such recommendations, to revise the rates, fees, and charges or 
Operating Expenses or methods of operation of the System and to take such other action as is in 
conformity with such recommendations to the extent the City feasibly may do so and to notify the 
B-25Trustee of the actions it has taken.  Upon the taking by the City of such actions, its failure to comply 
with the requirement described in paragraph (iii), above, will not constitute an Event of Default. 
(v) The City will permit the authorized represen tative of the Trustee, or of any Holder 
or Holders of 25% of the aggregate principal amount of the Bonds at the time Outstanding, to 
inspect the System and all records, accounts, a nd data relating to Revenues and the collection 
thereof, at all reasonable times. 
(vi) The City will not create nor suffer to be created any pledge, lien, or charge, except 
to secure Additional Bonds issued  in accordance herewith, that w ould constitute a pledge or lien 
prior to, or on a parity with, the pledge of and lien on Net Revenues created by the General Bond 
Ordinance and the Trust Agreement to secure the Bonds. 
(vii) The City will maintain a risk manage ment program that provides protection against 
risks of damage or destruction of the System a nd liabilities for the operations of the System.  In 
furtherance thereof, the City may, among other th ings:  self-insure in whole or in part; adopt 
alternative or supplemental risk management progr ams that the Council of the City determines to 
be reasonable; organize either solely or in connection with other political subdivisions, 
organizations or captive insurance companies; participate in programs of captive insurance 
companies organized by others; establish a self-insurance trust fund; participate in mutual or other 
cooperative insurance or other risk management programs or pools with other political subdivisions 
or organizations; participate in or enter into agreements with local, State or federal governments in 
order to achieve such insurance; or participate in  other alternative risk management programs.  In 
case of any damage to or destruction of any part of the System amounting to a loss of $500,000 or 
more, the City promptly must give or cause to  be given written notice thereof to the Trustee 
generally describing the nature and extent of such damage or destruction.  Regardless of whether 
the net proceeds of insurance, if any, receive d on account of such damage or destruction are 
sufficient for such purpose, the City promptly  will commence and complete, or cause to be 
commenced and completed, the repa ir or restoration of the System  as nearly as practicable to the 
value, condition and character thereof existing imme diately prior to such damage or destruction, 
with such changes or alterations, however, as the City may deem necessary for proper operation of 
the System and as will not impair or diminish, in the judgment of the City, the suitability of the 
System as a water pollution control system. 
(viii) The City will, for so long as any Bonds  are Outstanding, retain under the control 
of the City all facilities from time to time comp rising the System, subject to disposition in the 
ordinary course for substitution or  removal upon obsolescence, and will, in the exercise of such 
control, comply with all applicable requirements of law.  For purposes of the covenant described 
by this paragraph, the term “control” includes either the ownership or the operation of such facilities 
by the City. 
(ix) The City will observe and perform all its agreements and obligations provided for 
by any Outstanding Bonds, any Additional Bonds , the General Bond Ordinance or the Trust 
Agreement. 
(x) The City will, for each Fiscal Year, pr epare and adopt, within the time period and 
in a manner prescribed by law, a detailed budget of the estimated Revenues and Operating Expenses 
of the System.  The budget must provide for all operating Revenues, including interest income, and 
all Operating Expenses and other commitments required under the Trust Agreement. 
B-26(xi) The City will take whatever action ma y be reasonably required to enforce its rights 
against any Person collecting charges on behalf of the City for the use of the System and to protect 
the City’s interest in any funds collected by such Person that are payable to the City. 
Events of Default and Remedies 
The following constitute “Events of Default” under the Trust Agreement: 
(a) Default in the payment of any interest  on any Bond when and as the same becomes 
due and payable; 
(b) Default in the payment of the principal of (including any Sinking Fund 
Installments) or any redemption premium on a ny Bond when and as the same becomes due and 
payable, whether at the stated maturity or due date thereof, by acceleration or by call for redemption 
pursuant to any mandatory or optional redemption requirements; 
(c) Failure by the City to perform or observe any other covenant, agreement or 
condition on the part of the City contained in the General Bond Ordinance, any Supplemental Bond 
Ordinance, the Master Trust Agreement or any Supplemental Trust Agreement or in the Bonds 
(except if and to the extent that the City’s failure to perform or observe any such other covenant, 
agreement  or condition  is expressly stated not to constitute an Event of Default), which failure or 
default continues for a period of 60 days after written notice, by registered or certified mail, to the 
City specifying the failure or default and requiri ng the same to be remedied, which notice may be 
given by the Trustee in its discretion and which no tice must be given by the Trustee at the written 
request of the Holders of not less than 25% in aggregate principal amount of Bonds then 
Outstanding; and 
(d) Certain acts of insolvency involving the City. 
Upon the occurrence of an Event of Default descr ibed in paragraphs (a), (b) or (d) above, 
the Trustee may declare the principal of all Bonds th en Outstanding (if not then due and payable) and the 
interest accrued thereon to be due and payable immediately, whereupon that portion of the principal of the 
Bonds thereby coming due and the interest thereon accr ued to the date of payment will, without further 
action, become and be immediately due and payable.  If, after the occurrence of an Event of Default, the 
principal and interest has been thus declared due a nd payable because of such Event of Default, and prior 
to the entry of judgment in a court of law or equity for enforcement under the Trust Agreement or the 
appointment, and the confirmation thereof, of a receiver thereunder after an opportunity for hearing by the 
City, all sums payable under the Trust Agreement except the principal of, and interest accrued after the next 
preceding Interest Payment Date on, the Bonds which have not reached their stated maturity dates and 
which are due and payable solely by reason of that d eclaration, have been duly paid or provided for by 
deposit with the Trustee or Paying Agents, and all existing defaults have been made good, then and in every 
such case such payment or provision for payment will constitute a waiver of such Event of Default and its 
consequences and an automatic reces sion and annulment of such declaration, but no such waiver and 
rescission will extend to or affect a ny such subsequent Event of Default or impair any rights consequent 
thereon. 
Upon the occurrence of any Event of Default under the Trust Agreement, the Trustee, among other 
remedies, will be entitled to the appointment of a rece iver to administer and operate the System on behalf 
of the City, upon the filing of a suit to enforce the rights of the Trustee and the Holders of Bonds. 
B-27Application of Moneys Received Pursuant to Remedial Action 
All moneys received by the Trustee or receiver pur suant to any right given or action taken under 
the provisions the Trust Agreement will first be appl ied to the payment of the cost and expenses of the 
proceedings resulting in the collection of such mone ys and of the fees, expenses, liabilities and advances 
incurred or made by the Trustee or receiver.  The balan ce of such moneys will then be applied first to the 
payment, without priority or preference, of the interest on and principal or redemption premium of, if any, 
on the Bonds, in the manner set forth in the Trust Agreement. 
Rights and Remedies of Holders 
No Holder of any Bond will have any right to institute any suit, acti on or proceeding for the 
enforcement of the Trust Agreement or for the execution of any trust thereof or for the appointment of a 
receiver or any other remedy under the Trust Agreemen t unless an Event of Default has occurred and is 
continuing, such Holder has previously have given to  the Trustee written notice of such Event of Default, 
and the Holders of not less than 25% in aggregate principal amount of Bonds then Outstanding have made 
written request to the Trustee and have afforded the Trustee reasonable opportunity either to proceed to 
exercise the powers granted or to institute such acti on, suit or proceeding in its  own name and have also 
offered to the Trustee an indemnity as provided in the Trust Agreement, and the Trustee thereafter fails or 
refuses to exercise the powers granted under the Trust Ag reement, or to institute such action, suit or 
proceeding in its own name. 
Rights and Remedies Related to Other Secured Obligations 
In connection with the City’s entering into  any Interest Rate Hedge Agreement or 
Reimbursement Agreement or incurring or issuing an y Subordinated Indebtedness, a Supplemental Trust 
Agreement may amend or supplement the provisions of the Master Trust Agreement related to Events of 
Default and consequent rights and remedies to provide  for the protection and enforcement of the rights of 
the other party or parties to such Interest Rate Hedge Agreement or Reimbur sement Agreement or the 
holder or holders of such Subordinated Indebtedness and for the application of moneys to the payment of 
Parity Swap Obligations, Credit Obligations or debt service charges on Subordinated Indebtedness, 
provided that all such provisions must be consistent with the Master Trust Agreement and with the priorities 
of payment and security established hereby, and no such provision may diminish or derogate from the rights 
conferred on the Holders of Bonds and the priority of Bond Service Charges in a manner inconsistent with 
those priorities.  Without limiting the generality of the provision in the preceding sentence, no party entitled 
to the payment of Credit Obligations may be given the right, so long as any Bonds are outstanding or any 
Parity Swap Obligations are payable, to direct the acceleration of the maturity of any Bonds, nor may the 
holders of any Subordinated Indebtedness be given the right, so long as any Bonds are outstanding or any 
Parity Swap Obligations or Credit Obligations are payable, to direct the acceleration of the maturity of any 
Bonds.  The Trust Agreement provides that the provisions described in this paragraph will not be interpreted 
to limit the rights of Credit Providers to the enforcement of rights to payment of Bond Service Charges, nor 
may it be interpreted to limit the rights of parties entitled to the payment of Parity Swap Obligations to the 
enforcement of those rights. 
Supplemental Trust Agreements 
The Trust Agreement provides that the City and the Trustee may, without the consent of, or notice 
to, any of the Holders, enter into  a Supplemental Trust Agreement in connection with the issuance of 
Additional Bonds.  In addition, the City and the Trust ee may, without the consent of, or notice to, any of 
the Bondholders enter into Supplemental Trust Agreements  as may not, in the opinion of the City and the 
Trustee, be inconsistent with the terms and provisi ons of the Trust Agreement for any of the following 
B-28purposes:  (i) to cure any ambiguity, inconsistency or  formal defect or omission in the Master Trust 
Agreement or any Supplemental Trust Agreement; (ii) to grant to or confer upon the Trustee for the benefit 
of the Bondholders any additional rights, remedies, powers or authority that may lawfully be granted to or 
conferred upon the Bondholders or the Trustee; (iii) to subject additional revenues or receipts to the pledge 
of the Trust Agreement; (iv) to add to the covenants and agreements of the City contained in the Trust 
Agreement other covenants and agreements thereafter to be observed for the protection of the Bondholders, 
or to surrender or limit any right, power or authority reserved to or conferred upon the City in the Master 
Trust Agreement, including the limitation of rights of redemption so that in certain instances Bonds of 
different Series will be retained in some prescribed relation to one another; (v) to evidence any succession 
to the City and the assumption by such successors of th e covenants and agreements of the City contained 
in the Master Trust Agreement and the Bonds; (vi) to  permit the exchange of Bonds, at the option of the 
Holders thereof, for coupon Bonds of the same series  payable to bearer, in an aggregate principal amount 
not exceeding the unmatured and unredeemed principal amount of the Predecessor Bonds, bearing interest 
at the same rate or rates and maturing on the same da te or dates, with coupons attached representing all 
unpaid interest due or to become due thereon if, in the opinion of Bond Counsel, that exchange would not 
result in the interest on any of the Bonds Outstanding becoming subject to federal income taxation; (vii) to 
permit the use of a Book-Entry system to identify the ow ner of an interest in an obligation issued by the 
City under the Trust Agreement, whether that obligation was formerly, or could be, evidenced by a tangible 
security; (viii) to permit the Trustee to comply with any obligations imposed upon it by law; (ix) to specify 
further the duties and responsibilities of, and to define  further the relationship among, the Trustee, the 
Registrar and any Paying Agents; (x) to achieve comp liance of the Trust Agreement with any applicable 
federal securities or tax law; (xi) to make any change necessary to obtain or maintain a rating on any of the 
Bonds by a Rating Service; and (xii) to make any othe r change to insert any provision into or delete or 
amend any provision of the Trust Agreement, provided that such insertion, deletion or amendment will not 
adversely affect the rating (other than any rati ng based upon credit enhancement or liquidity support 
provided by any party other than the City, which may not be taken into account for purposes of the clause 
described by this paragraph) then assigned to any Bonds Outstanding by any Rating Agency. 
All other Supplemental Trust Agreements must be approved by the Holders of not less than 51% 
in aggregate principal amount of the Bonds then outst anding (excluding Bonds then held or owned by the 
City); provided that a Supplemental Trust Agreemen t permitting (i) an extension of the maturity of the 
principal of or the interest on any Bond, or a reduction in the principal amount of any Bonds or the rate of 
interest or redemption premium thereon, or a reduc tion in the amount or extension of the time of any 
payment required by any mandatory sinking fund requirements, may not be entered into without the consent 
of the Holder of each Bond so affected or (ii) a reduction in the aggregate principal amount of the Bonds 
required for consent to such Supplemental Trust Agreements, may not be entered into without the consent 
of the Holders of all of the Bonds then outstanding. 
Defeasance 
If the City pays or causes to be paid all principal,  redemption premium, if any, and interest due or 
to become due on the Bonds, and provision is made for paying all other sums payable by the City under the 
Trust Agreement, the Trustee will release and discharge the Trust Agreement.  All Outstanding Bonds will 
be deemed to have been paid or caused to be paid within the meanin g of the Trust Agreement if (i) the 
Trustee and any Paying Agents hold, in trust for and irrevocably committed thereto, sufficient moneys, or 
(ii) the Trustee will hold, in trust for and irrevocably committed thereto, Defeasance Obligations which are 
of such maturities and interest payment dates and bear such interest as will, without further investment or 
reinvestment of either the principal amount thereof or the interest earnings therefrom, be sufficient together 
with moneys referred to in clause (i) above, for the pa yment, at their maturity or redemption date, of all 
principal, redemption premium, if any, and interest  thereof and thereon to the date of maturity or 
redemption, as the case may be, or if default in such payment has occurred on such date then to the date of 
B-29the tender of such payment; provided, that if any Bonds are to be redeemed prior to the maturity thereof, 
notice of such redemption must have been duly given or provision satisfactory to the Trustee have been 
duly made for the giving of such notice. 
The Trustee 
The Trustee agrees in the Trust Agreement to pe rform the trusts imposed upon it in the Trust 
Agreement as an ordinarily prudent trustee under a trust agreement.  The Trust Agreement provides that 
the Trustee may act upon the opinion or advice of any attorney and will not be responsible for any loss or 
damage resulting from any action taken or not taken in good faith reliance upon such opinion or advice.  In 
addition, the Trust Agreement provides that the Trustee will be protected in acting upon certain documents 
believed to be genuine and correct and to have been signed or sent by the proper persons. 
Extent of City’s Covenants; No Personal Liability 
All covenants, stipulations, obligations and ag reements of the City contained in the Trust 
Agreement will be deemed to be covenants, stipulations, obligations and agreements of the City to the full 
extent authorized by the Ohio Revised Code and permitted by the Constitution of the State and the Charter 
of the City.  No covenant, stipula tion, obligation or agreement contai ned in the Trust Agreement will be 
deemed to be a covenant, stipula tion, obligation or agreement of any present or future member of the 
Council of the City or agent or employee of the City  in his or her individual capacity, and neither the 
members of the Council of the City nor any official  executing the Bonds will be liable personally on the 
Bonds or be subject to any personal liability or accountability by reason of the issuance thereof.

FORM OF BOND COUNSEL OPINION 
August 15, 2024 
To: City of Cleveland, Ohio 
Stifel, Nicolaus & Company, Incorporated 
Zions Bank, a Division of ZB, National Association, as Trustee 
We have served as bond counsel to our client the City of Cleveland, Ohio (the “City”) in 
connection with the issuance by the City of its $29,675,000 Water Pollution Control Revenue 
Bonds, Series 2024 (the “Series 2024 Bonds”), dated the date of this letter.   
The Series 2024 Bonds are issued pursuant to the authority of the Constitution and laws of 
the State of Ohio, including Article XVIII of th e Ohio Constitution, the Charter of the City, and 
Ordinances No. 29-16 (the “G eneral Bond Ordinance”) and No. 898-2023 (the “Series 2024 
Ordinance”), passed by the Council of the City on January 25, 2016 and September 18, 2023, 
respectively, and under the Master Trust Agreem ent, dated April 14, 2016, which includes the 
General Bond Ordinance (together , the “Master Trust Agreemen t”), as supplemented by the 
Second Supplemental Trust Agreement, dated August 15, 2024, which includes the Series 2024 
Ordinance (the “Second Supplemen tal Trust Agreement” and toge ther with the Master Trust 
Agreement, as heretofore supplemented and amended, the “Trust Agreement”), each between the 
City and Zions Bank, a Division of ZB, National Association, as truste e (the “Trustee”).  
Capitalized terms not otherwise defined in this letter are used as defined in the Trust Agreement. 
In our capacity as bond counsel, we have examin ed the transcript of proceedings relating 
to the issuance of the Series 2024 Bonds, a copy of the signed and authenticated Series 2024 Bond 
of the first maturity, the Trust Agreement and such other documents, matters and law as we deem 
necessary to render the opinions set forth in this letter. 
Based on that examination and subject to the limitations stated below, we are of the opinion 
that under existing law:  
1. The Series 2024 Bonds a nd the Trust Agreement are valid and binding obligations of 
the City enforceable in accordance with their respective terms. 
2. The Series 2024 Bonds constitute special obligations of the City, and the principal 
of and interest on (collectively, “debt service”) the Series 2024 Bonds, together with 
debt service on any other obligations issued and outstanding on a parity with the 
Series 2024 Bonds, from time to time, under the Master Trust Agreement, are 
payable from and secured solely by the Net Revenues and Special Funds 
established under the Master Trust Agreem ent, all as described in the Trust 
Agreement.  The payment of debt service on the Series 2024 Bonds is not secured 
by an obligation or pledge of any money raised by taxation, and the Series 2024 
Bonds do not represent or constitute a general obligation debt of the City or a pledge 
C-1of the faith and credit of the City, the State of Ohio or any of its political 
subdivisions. 
3. Interest on the Series 2024 Bonds is excluded from gross income for federal income 
tax purposes under Section 103 of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended, 
and is not an item of tax preference for purposes of the federal alternative minimum 
tax imposed on individuals.  Interest on, and any profit made on the sale, exchange or 
other disposition of, the Series 2024 Bonds are exempt from all Ohio state and local 
taxation, except the estate tax, the domes tic insurance company tax, the dealers in 
intangibles tax, the tax levied on the basis of the total equity capital of financial 
institutions, and the net worth base of the corporate franchise tax.  We express no 
opinion as to any other tax consequences regarding the Series 2024 Bonds. 
The opinions stated above are based on an analysis of existing laws , regulations, rulings 
and court decisions and cover certain matters not directly addressed by such authorities.  In 
rendering all such opinions we assume, without independent verification, and rely upon (i) the 
accuracy of the factual matters represented, wa rranted or certified in the proceedings and 
documents we have examined a nd (ii) the due and le gal authorization, execution and delivery of 
those documents by, and the valid, binding and enforceable nature of those documents upon, any 
parties other than the City. 
We express no opinion herein regarding the prio rity of the lien on Net Revenues, Special 
Funds or other funds created by the Master Trust Agreement. 
In rendering those opinions with respect to th e treatment of the interest on the Series 2024 
Bonds under the federal tax laws, we further assume and rely upon compliance with the covenants 
in the proceedings and documents  we have examined, including those of the City.  Failure to 
comply with certain of those covenants subsequent to issuance of the Series 2024 Bonds may cause 
interest on the Series 2024 Bonds to be included in gross income for federal income tax purposes 
retroactively to their date of issuance. 
The rights of the owners of the Series 2024 Bonds and the enforceability of the Series 2024 
Bonds and the Trust Agreement are subject to bankruptcy, insolvency, reorganization, moratorium, 
fraudulent conveyance or transfer, and other laws relating to or af fecting the rights and remedies 
of creditors generally; to the application of equitable principles, wh ether considered in a 
proceeding at law or in equity; to the exercise of judicial discretion; and to limitations on legal 
remedies against public entities. 
No opinions other than those expressly stated herein are implied or shall be inferred as a 
result of anything contained in or omitted from this letter. The opinions expressed in this letter are 
stated only as of the time of its delivery, and we disclaim any obligation to revise or supplement 
this letter thereafter. Our engagement as bond counsel in connection with the original issuance and 
delivery of the Series 2024 Bonds is concluded upon delivery of this letter. 
Respectfully submitted,

CONTINUING DISCLOSURE CERTIFICATE 
This CONTINUING DISCLOSURE CERTIFICATE, dated as of August 15, 2024 (the 
“Certificate”), is made, signed and delivered by the CITY OF CLEVELAND, OHIO , a 
municipal corporation and political subdivision duly organized and existing under its Charter and 
the Constitution and laws of the State of Ohio (the “City”), for the bene fit of the Holders and 
Beneficial Owners (as defined herein) from time to time of the City’s $29,675,000 Water Pollution 
Control Revenue Bonds, Series 2024 (the “Serie s 2024 Bonds”), authorized by Ordinance Nos. 
29-16 and 898-2023, each passed on January 25, 2016 and September 18, 2023, respectively 
(collectively the “Bond Ordinance”). 
RECITALS 
The City, by passage of the Bond Ordinance, has determined to issue the Series 2024 Bonds 
to provide funds for City purposes, and S tifel, Nicholas & Comp any, Incorporated, as 
representative of the underwriters identified in the Bond Purchase Agreement, dated August 1, 
2024 (collectively, the “Participating Underwriter”), has agreed to provide those funds to the City 
by purchasing the Series 2024 Bonds.  As a cond ition to the purchase of the Series 2024 Bonds 
from the City and the sale of the Series 2024 Bonds to Holders and Beneficial Owners, the 
Participating Underwriter is requ ired to reasonably determine that  the City has undertaken, in a 
written agreement for the benefit of Holders and Beneficial  Owners of the Series 2024 Bonds, to 
provide certain information in accordance with the Rule (as defined herein). 
NOW, THEREFORE, in accordance with the Bond Ordi nance, the City covenants and 
agrees as set forth in this Continuing Disclosure Certificate. 
SECTION 1. Purpose of Continuing Disclosure Certificate .  This Certificate is 
being entered into, signed and delivered for the be nefit of the Holders and Beneficial Owners of 
the Series 2024 Bonds and in order to assist the Participating Underwriter of the Series 2024 Bonds 
in complying with Rule 15c2-12(b)(5) promulgated by the Securities and Exchange Commission 
(SEC) pursuant to the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as may be amended from time to time (the 
“Rule”).

capitalized terms shall have the following meanings in this Certificate, unless the context clearly 
otherwise requires.  Reference to “Sections” shall mean sections of this Certificate. 
“Annual Filing” means any Annual Info rmation Filing provided by the City 
pursuant to, and as described in, Sections 3 and 4. 
“Audited Financial Statements” means the audited basic financial statements of the 
Water Pollution Control Division (the “Division”) of the City, prepared in conformity with 
generally accepted accounting principles. 
D-1“Beneficial Owner” means any person that (a) has the power, directly or indirectly, 
to vote or consent with respect to, or to dispose of ownership of, any Series 2024 Bonds 
(including persons holding Series 2024 Bonds  through nominees, depositories or other 
intermediaries), or (b) is treated as the owner of any Series 2024 Bonds for federal income 
tax purposes. 
“Division” means the Division of Water Pollution Control, a division of the City’s 
Department of Public Utilities. 
“EMMA” means the Electronic Municipal Market Access system of the MSRB; 
information regarding submissions to EMMA is available at http://emma.msrb.org. 
“Filing Date” means the last day of the ninth month following the end of each Fiscal 
Year (or the next succeeding business day if that day is not a bus iness day), beginning 
September 30, 2025. 
“Financial Obligation” m eans a (a) debt obligation, (b) derivative instrument 
entered into in connection with, or pledged as  security or a source of payment for, an 
existing or planned debt oblig ation, or (c) guarantee of an obligation or instrument 
described in either clause (a) or (b).  Financial Obligation shall not include municipal 
securities as to which a final official statement has been provided to the MSRB consistent 
with the Rule. 
“Fiscal Year” means the 12-month period be ginning on January 1 of each year or 
such other 12-month period as the Division shall adopt as its fiscal year. 
“Holder” means, with respect to the Series 2024 Bonds, the person in whose name 
a Series 2024 Bond is registered in accordance with the Trust Agreement.

being sold in an offering document (such as the Official Statement); the City is the only

August 1, 2024. 
“Participating Underwriter” means any of the original underwriters of the Series 
2024 Bonds required to comply with the Rule in connection with offering of the Series 
2024 Bonds.
